          The 50 Greatest Video Game Athletes of All Time (with Video)

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            You have lost friends, punched siblings, broken televisions, smashed controllers, destroyed game consoles, snapped discs, kicked holes in the wall, and you might have even broken a bone.
           </p>
           <p>
            Video games bring out the worst in us. Especially because of the following 50 virtual athletes.
           </p>
           <p>
            They can run circles around your defenses, hit three pointers at will, score goals from behind the blue line, and hit 900-foot home runs. You love to play with them, but you cringe at the thought of playing against them.
           </p>
          </div>
          <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Begin Slideshow">
           Begin Slideshow

           </span>
          </a>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             50. Shaq: NBA Jam
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:256px">
            <img alt="50. Shaq: NBA Jam" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/446/Nbajamte_shaq1_crop_256x224.png?1286987703" height="224" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="256"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Shaq was built for NBA Jam.
           </p>
           <p>
            His mammoth size, dunking power, and blocking abilities made him one of the game's elite. The Big Diesel and teammate Penny Hardaway made for a lethal duo. Hardaway's athleticism allowed for Shaq to draw one on one matchups, which were a cake walk for the Shaqtus.
           </p>
           <p>
            And if you were playing against, you were better off trying to chuck up three pointers, because Shaq would not allow you to dunk on him.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="640">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/jpVWs3N-mSQ?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/jpVWs3N-mSQ?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="640">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-3 cf display-none " data-page="3">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             49. Larry Bird: NBA 2k3
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:224px">
            <img alt="49. Larry Bird: NBA 2k3" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/432/nba2k3_legends3_640w_crop_224x398_original.jpg?1286987053" height="398" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="224"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            In 2003, NBA 2k decided to pay homage to the game's greats by including them in NBA 2K3. There was a whole lineup of legends and legendary teams to choose from, but one stood about above the rest.
           </p>
           <p>
            Larry Bird was unstoppable on the virtual hardwood. He could hit threes at will, pull up and drain and jumper regardless of who was guarding him, and he could force his way into the paint and lay in a finger roll with ease.
           </p>
           <p>
            Larry Legend had a short stint in the video game world, but he made it count.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             48. Devin Hester: Madden 2008/2009
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:380px">
            <img alt="48. Devin Hester: Madden 2008/2009" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/434/407/madden09hesterfgreturn2a_crop_380x189.jpg?1286565851" height="189" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="380"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Devin Hester burst into NFL stardom after a return-touchdown-studded 2007 rookie season. Hester's prowess was so electrifying, that the folks at Madden did the previously unthinkable. They gave Hester a 100 speed rating.
           </p>
           <p>
            This marked the first time in Madden history that any player was given a 100 rating in any category. Needless to say, the effects were friendly on Bears fans, and very annoying to everybody playing against them.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/9J2NKSpr20o?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/9J2NKSpr20o?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             47. Brian Moorman: Madden
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:594px">
            <img alt="47. Brian Moorman: Madden" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/372/Moorman_crop_594x420.jpg?1286904741" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="594"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Who says punters can't be awesome in video games?
           </p>
           <p>
            OK, so Brian Moorman might not classify as "awesome," but considering he has speed ratings in the 80s, he makes for a deadly weapon. Fake punts become an option every time he trots out for a kick, and his speed allows for effective fake field goals as well.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/no-7bq_VHrg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/no-7bq_VHrg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             46. Sammy Sosa: Triple Play Baseball 2000
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:450px">
            <img alt="46. Sammy Sosa: Triple Play Baseball 2000" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/428/Sammy-Sosa_crop_450x300.jpg?1286904970" height="300" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="450"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            962 foot home runs.
           </p>
           <p>
            Isn't this all of the proof we need that Slammin' Sammy was juicing?
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             45. Shawn Kemp: NBA Jam
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:320px">
            <img alt="45. Shawn Kemp: NBA Jam" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/503/nba-jam-tournament-edition-screenshot-002_crop_320x280.png?1286838305" height="280" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="320"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            In his prime, Seattle Supersonics star Shawn Kemp was one of the NBA's most devastating dunkers. Kemp had godly power above the rim and he was not afraid to throw down on anybody who dared step in his way.
           </p>
           <p>
            So, naturally, Kemp was a superstar in NBA Jam, a game centered almost entirely on slam dunks.
           </p>
           <p>
            Kemp was virtually impossible to stop once he went up for a dunk. His defensive mastery was on par as well. Kemp, as this video shows, was a lock down defender and a ball hawk. He could easily snatch the ball from anybody.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/sEYctRuoOkM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/sEYctRuoOkM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             44. Tim Tebow: NCAA Football 2010
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:500px">
            <img alt="44. Tim Tebow: NCAA Football 2010" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/430/ncaa10tebow_crop_500x220.jpg?1286905486" height="220" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="500"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Although Tebow spent his entire college tenure as a total media darling, his NCAA Football characters never reached the status many Gator fans hoped they would.
           </p>
           <p>
            Still, Tebow's size, speed, and throw power combination allowed him to serve as the games best quarterback, and arguably its best player in NCAA Football 2010. Tebow could truck any defender, and Florida's playbook created some unstoppable plays for the QB.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/jXZqttsn3R8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/jXZqttsn3R8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             43. Tom Chambers: Lakers Versus Celtics and The NBA Playoffs
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:540px">
            <img alt="43. Tom Chambers: Lakers Versus Celtics and The NBA Playoffs " data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/796/chambers_bulls_540_crop_540x275.jpg?1286915462" height="275" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="540"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Tom Chambers had a very underrated and undervalued career. He was an integral player on several contenders, a four-time All-Star, and even a one-time All-Star Game MVP.
           </p>
           <p>
            Most importantly, though, Chambers is the best white dunker of all time. His skill has, for one reason or another, fallen largely by the wayside, but mastery is well documented in Lakers versus Celtics and the NBA Playoffs.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/NfWWyLWbKtM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/NfWWyLWbKtM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             42. Wayne Gretzky: Wayne Gretzky's 3D Hockey
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:294px">
            <img alt="42. Wayne Gretzky: Wayne Gretzky's 3D Hockey" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/813/Wayne_Gretzky_Biography_crop_294x420.jpg?1286916745" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="294"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Easily one of the most underrated sports games of all time, Wayne Gretzky 3D Hockey allowed you to pants your opponent, literally turn your goaltender into a brick wall, and ignite the opposing team's goal into flames.
           </p>
           <p>
            Not surprisingly, the greatest player in hockey history was incredible in his own video game. He had arguably the greatest speed and the hardest shot in the game.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/t3A1hMAVbwg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             </param>

             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/t3A1hMAVbwg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             41. Tom Brady: Madden 2009
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:560px">
            <img alt="41. Tom Brady: Madden 2009" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/441/629/Tom-Brady-Madden-560x315_crop_560x315.jpg?1286945934" height="315" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="560"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Although football's golden boy is yet to surpass Peyton Manning's mastery of the Madden ranks, he has had some wicked awesome virtual characters.
           </p>
           <p>
            Tom Brady made arguably his most dominant appearance in Madden 2009. The Patriots spread offense scheme made them almost impossible to stop, and the constant threat of Randy Moss breaking free on a fly route forced you to play conservative.
           </p>
           <p>
            Brady could make pinpoint accurate throws across his body, on the run, and in the pocket. He never missed his receivers.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/sYtJ7YWuy88?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             40. Nolan Ryan: Nolan Ryan's Baseball
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="40. Nolan Ryan: Nolan Ryan's Baseball" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/498/nolan-ryan_crop_630x420.jpg?1286833784" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Anytime a video game is named after an athlete, he is guaranteed to be virtually unbeatable. But when that athlete is the greatest pitcher in baseball pitcher, he is really unbeatable.
           </p>
           <p>
            Ryan consistently tossed heat in the upper 90s, making defeating the computer a cakewalk.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             39. David Ortiz: MLB 06 The Show
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="39. David Ortiz: MLB 06 The Show" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/245/mlb-06-the-show-20051129114858373_640w_crop_630x420.jpg?1286984755" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Big Papi might have been juicing around the time he graced the cover of MLB '06 The Show, but there's no denying how incredibly dominant he was on the virtual diamond.
           </p>
           <p>
            Ortiz had insane power, and he could smack home runs off of nearly any pitch. Low and away, high and in, or right down the middle, you were better off just putting him on base.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="640">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/SlvJxUkyy_E?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             38. Vince Young: NCAA Football 2006
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:300px">
            <img alt="38. Vince Young: NCAA Football 2006" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/212/vinceyoung_crop_300x400.jpg?1286984126" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="300"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Vince Young's virtual character in NCAA Football 06 represents a whole breed of unstoppable players. For the entirety of its existence, NCAA Football has failed to address the problem of the dual threat quarterback.
           </p>
           <p>
            Basically, if you have a scrambling quarterback in any NCAA game, you become almost impossible to stop. So, naturally, the best scrambling quarterback of the past decade, Vince Young, was a superstar in the game. His size, speed, and rocket arm proved overwhelming for anybody playing against him. If you were unfortunate enough to play against him, you're only hope was to keep up on the scoreboard, because you were not going to stop him.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/5EnnRxBJ0oM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/5EnnRxBJ0oM?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             37. Reggie Bush: Madden 2007
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:200px">
            <img alt="37. Reggie Bush: Madden 2007" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/413/bush_NFL_crop_200x175.jpg?1286830525" height="175" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="200"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Reggie Bush hype reached ridiculous levels as his illustrious collegiate career drew to a close. Once Bush landed with the Saints, not even the folks at Madden could resist the hype.
           </p>
           <p>
            Bush was granted an 87 overall rating, making him almost as deadly as his NCAA Football 2006 character. He could not quite pull off the superhuman jukes in Madden, but he could still outrun most defenders in the game.
           </p>
           <p>
            Even though Bush-hysteria has died down a little bit, he will enjoy a fruitful career of great video game characters due to his elusive traits.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/9oWtAsRxR34?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/9oWtAsRxR34?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             36. Dominik Hasek: NHL 2K4
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:350px">
            <img alt="36. Dominik Hasek: NHL 2K4" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/175/nhl02_display_image_crop_350x342.jpg?1286982828" height="342" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="350"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            It's only fitting that "The Dominator" is the only goaltender to make this list.
           </p>
           <p>
            In  NHL 2K4, Hasek was a truly unique player that hockey video games have  failed to replicate. Hockey games are generally geared toward scoring  goals to keep players excited and intrigued. Today, regardless of how  good the opposing goaltender may be, you can generally score cliche  goals.
           </p>
           <p>
            Against Hasek, however, nothing worked. He could try all of  the one timer, cross ice, slap shot, wrist shot, or double deke moves.  He was a brick wall.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/HVOeJYswGbE?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/HVOeJYswGbE?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-17 cf display-none " data-page="17">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>

             </a>
             <div class="paginators_counter">
              17
              <span class="br-light-grey">
               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">
               52
              </span>
             </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             35. Didier Drogba: 2010 FIFA World Cup South Africa
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:418px">
            <img alt="35. Didier Drogba: 2010 FIFA World Cup South Africa " data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/852/drogba--article_image_crop_418x275.jpg?1286916654" height="275" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="418"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            As video games enhance and advance, it becomes increasingly difficult for virtual players to stand out as commanding and dominant.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, last summer, Didier Drogba broke the trend. Drogba's power was unparalleled in 2010 FIFA World Cup South Africa. If he had the ball on a breakaway, there was no way your defender could either catch up to him or out-power him for possession of the ball.
           </p>
           <p>
            Not to mention, Drogba had an absolute rocket-shot, allowing him to score from ridiculous distances and spots on the pitch.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="640">

           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             34. Donovan McNabb: Madden 2006 / NFL 2K5
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:327px">
            <img alt="34. Donovan McNabb: Madden 2006 / NFL 2K5" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/972/1114031394_crop_327x405.jpg?1286919717" height="405" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="327"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            If you failed to trade for or draft Michael Vick in a Madden fantasy draft, Donovan McNabb was probably your second choice. McNabb did not possess Vick-like speed, but he was not too far behind.
           </p>
           <p>
            Donovan still had a lethal combination of speed and arm strength and accuracy, which made him one of the deadliest and most valuable players in both Madden 2006 and NFL 2K5. Philadelphia's trio of McNabb, Terrell Owens, and Brian Westbrook made the Eagles a small-scale juggernaut in 2005.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/12J7bJM6mG4?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/12J7bJM6mG4?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-19 cf display-none " data-page="19">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             33. Ichiro: MLB 09: The Show
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:472px">
            <img alt="33. Ichiro: MLB 09: The Show  " data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/184/ichiro472_crop_472x238.jpg?1286983304" height="238" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="472"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Despite almost a decade of unparalleled consistency, Ichiro has become one of sport's most under-appreciated athletes.
           </p>
           <p>
            The same does not necessarily ring true for virtual Ichiro, however.
           </p>
           <p>
            Ichiro can make contact on almost anything thrown at him, he can easily lay down perfect bunt singles, or he can smack a ball into the gap. Similarly, Ichiro's speed makes him a lock to grab a stolen base, and his rocket arm forces you to play your base runners conservatively. When you're playing Ichiro, he's in your head.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/NQwqemfBaQA?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/NQwqemfBaQA?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             32. Brett Favre: NFL QB Club '99
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:300px">
            <img alt="32. Brett Favre: NFL QB Club '99" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/405/brett-favre_crop_300x300.jpg?1286830105" height="300" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="300"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            If you thought John Madden was the only person who has intimate feelings for Favre, you were wrong.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apparently the producers of the N64 football game, NFL QB Club did as well.
           </p>
           <p>
            Not only did Favre grace the cover of the game for five straight years, but he was a force to be reckoned with. Understandably, Favre could toss the pigskin around with great accuracy and velocity, but things got a little bit out of hand once he stepped out of the pocket and looked like Tecmo Bowl Bo Jackson.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/aZib1PhPE9c?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/aZib1PhPE9c?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             31. LeBron James: NBA Live 08
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:380px">
            <img alt="31. LeBron James: NBA Live 08" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/652/ljamesnbalive08a_crop_380x190.jpg?1286839398" height="190" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="380"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            LeBron James has yet to hit his stride in the video game world. That is not to say he has not been great, but he is yet to find his signature game. Teamed up with Dwyane Wade and Chris Bosh, LeBron's character in NBA 2K11 might achieve greatness, but we'll have let time decide his fate.
           </p>
           <p>
            Anyway, LBJ has still been represented very well in video games over the years. His overpowering size and speed makes him unstoppable to most defenders, and his ability to step back and hit a shot makes him the best player in most basketball games.
           </p>
           <p>
            In NBA Live 08, things got a little bit ridiculous for Bron Bron. With the ball in his hands, he was almost a mortal lock to score. James could dunk over anybody, and he could do it in style.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/YSn7G_8KQp8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/YSn7G_8KQp8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             30. Terrell Owens: NFL 2k5
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:350px">
            <img alt="30. Terrell Owens: NFL 2k5" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/485/owens_display_image_crop_350x263.jpg?1286833570" height="263" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="350"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The only thing that is truly unrealistic about NFL 2K5 Terrell Owens is the postgame interview he gives in this video. "We really performed well offensively, ran our plays cleanly, and everybody did their part." Doesn't sound like T.O. to me. This is more like it, "I played great today, did my part and scored a touchdown. Everybody else needs to step their games up though."
           </p>
           <p>
            Beyond that, however, Owens was a commanding figure in the game, especially when paired up with quarterback Donovan McNabb. Owens could outrun most any defensive back and haul in a deep pass, or he could take a short pass, shed a tackle or two, and sprint into the end zone.
           </p>
           <p>
            T.O. was the best receiver in the NFL circa 2005, and fittingly, was the best receiver in this game.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/81btVVc1diI?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/81btVVc1diI?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             29. Marshall Faulk: Madden 2003
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:395px">
            <img alt="29. Marshall Faulk: Madden 2003" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/441/018/Madden2003_crop_395x277.jpg?1286945422" height="277" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="395"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Marshall Faulk may have fallen victim to the Madden curse after landing the cover spot in 2003, but he made his days as the game's best running back count.
           </p>
           <p>
            Faulk had blazing speed and ankle-breaking jukes. Most vital to his success, though, was his reliability on swing and screen passes. Getting Faulk into space usually equated to touchdowns or massive gains.
           </p>
           <p>
            And it didn't exactly hurt that the Rams offense featured Kurt Warner, Isaac Bruce and Torry Holt.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/Dh_3ByZHNa0?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/Dh_3ByZHNa0?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             28. Kobe Bryant: NBA 2k10
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="28. Kobe Bryant: NBA 2k10" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/655/Perfect-Kobe-Bryant-Patches-for-Nba-2k10-1_crop_630x420.jpg?1286839473" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Considering Kobe Bryant dominates the NBA ranks at will, it's no surprise that his video game character is dominant on the virtual hardwood. Basketball video games still seem to allow for uber-dominant players, and Kobe fits that pedigree.
           </p>
           <p>
            Kobe was deadly from basically everywhere on the court, particularly once he had the ball on a fastbreak. He could also hit almost any shot from behind the arc, making him a force to the reckoned with.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/Hm8pAGkiBxY?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/Hm8pAGkiBxY?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             27. Pavel Bure: NHL '94 / '95
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:310px">
            <img alt="27. Pavel Bure: NHL '94 / '95" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/837/PavelBure-close-up_crop_310x420.jpg?1286916313" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="310"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Time passes, but one video game law remains the same: Speed kills.
           </p>
           <p>
            In NHL 95, Pavel Bure possessed god-like speed and was therefore god-like in his play. With the puck on his stick, Bure could weave through or around defenders, creating breakaways and easy goal scoring opportunities.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/L4NcYL6TD3I?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/L4NcYL6TD3I?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             26. Walter Payton: Tecmo Bowl
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:466px">
            <img alt="26. Walter Payton: Tecmo Bowl" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/371/2009_09_16_payton_crop_466x420.jpg?1286904448" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="466"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            It only makes sense that the best running back in NFL history dominate the virtual ranks as well.
           </p>
           <p>
            Sweetness was not quite on par with Bo Jackson or Christian Okoye, but the man was still nearly impossible to stop.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/ENfUFp2btL8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed src="http://www.youtube.com/v/ENfUFp2btL8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             25. Reggie Bush: NCAA Football 2006
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="25. Reggie Bush: NCAA Football 2006" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/434/415/bush1_crop_630x294.jpg?1286566249" height="294" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Reggie Bush's dominance at USC translated believably into NCAA Football 2006. Bush flashed spin moves and juke moves that few others players could, and was equally as threatening offensively as he was returning kicks.
           </p>
           <p>
            Unfortunately, because of the recent sanctions involving Bush, the NCAA has essentially erased all records and remnants of his collegiate career. So, it looks like virtual Reggie Bush is now the last remaining evidence of the running back's glory days at USC.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/m7hNBl7CeOo?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/m7hNBl7CeOo?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             24. Shaq: NBA Live 2005
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:459px">
            <img alt="24. Shaq: NBA Live 2005" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/441/673/nba-live-06-power-players-20050728045245195-000-000_crop_459x297.jpg?1286946413" height="297" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="459"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            He could stuff the crap out of anybody, and he could throw down emotionally scarring dunks on anybody.
           </p>
           <p>
            If Shaq  was on any of your video game basketball teams since 1996, there's a  good chance you crushed your opponent. O' Neal has been so dominant  throughout the duration of his virtual career that he essentially forced  your opponents to rely on perimeter shots.
           </p>
           <p>
            Kobe and Dwayne Wade  only further accentuated his stature. He could easily set them up for  wide open three pointers, or feed them wide open alley oops.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/aUvBQGPGhS8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/aUvBQGPGhS8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             23. Allen Iverson: NBA 2k3
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:300px">
            <img alt="23. Allen Iverson: NBA 2k3" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/643/espn-nba-basketball-3_crop_300x225.jpg?1286839065" height="225" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="300"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Allen Iverson had the perfect video game athlete DNA.
           </p>
           <p>
            He played point guard, a position often relied on for a majority of scoring in NBA video games. He had lightning quickness, smooth ball handling skills, a deadly jumper, and a knack for getting to the hoop and drawing fouls.
           </p>
           <p>
            Iverson landed on the cover of NBA 2K3, and made his presence felt. His speed was too much for defenders to handle. He could easily go coast to coast by just running around or crossing over defenders, and then finish the play with a signature finger roll.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="640">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/J58mO0h-6rg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/J58mO0h-6rg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="640">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             22. Barry Sanders: Madden 1998
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:317px">
            <img alt="22. Barry Sanders: Madden 1998" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/474/44619_0_org_crop_317x280.jpg?1286833080" height="280" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="317"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Short, shifty, preposterous speed, and inconceivable juke moves summarizes Barry Sanders' running style. It also summarizes the perfect blend of attributes for a great video game football player.
           </p>
           <p>
            Oddly, virtual Barry Sanders never quite found a niche or signature game like so many other video game athletes of his time did. Madden 98 stands out to most as the game Sanders stood out in, but he hardly reached legendary status there.
           </p>
           <p>
            It looks like he just fell through the cracks in the video game world, but that should not diminish the greatness he still displayed. There's no evidence of Sanders' in Madden 98 on the Internet, but this video does him a little bit of justice.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/6QmEVhC_LKc?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/6QmEVhC_LKc?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             21. Adrian Peterson: NCAA Football 2007
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:459px">
            <img alt="21. Adrian Peterson: NCAA Football 2007" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/659/ncaa-football-07-top-25-half-backs-20060606041921437-000_crop_459x311.jpg?1286902579" height="311" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="459"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            If you'll notice this photo, Adrian Peterson is starting his touchdown celebration at the 50 yard line. This is because he knows damn well that he's going to score. And if you were playing against Peterson in NCAA Football 2007, you knew he was too.
           </p>
           <p>
            Peterson was an absolute workhorse in NCAA '07. He could steamroll any defenders, or he could just run by them. Check out his ratings:
            <strong>
            </strong>
           </p>
           <p>
            <strong>
             Overall:
            </strong>
            98
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Speed:
            </strong>
            93
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Strength:
            </strong>
            80
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Awareness:
            </strong>
            87
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Agility:
            </strong>
            92
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Acceleration:
            </strong>
            96
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Catch:
            </strong>
            62
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Carry:
            </strong>
            97
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Jump:
            </strong>
            84
            <br/>
            <strong>
             Break Tackle:
            </strong>
            98
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             20. Michael Jordan: NBA 2K11
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:236px">
            <img alt="20. Michael Jordan: NBA 2K11" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/470/nba-2k11-20100813024136153-000_crop_236x420.jpg?1286832703" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="236"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Michael Jordan is coming out of retirement again! Sort of.
           </p>
           <p>
            M.J. is gracing the cover of NBA 2K11, a game which is already being hailed as legendary. Because of its recent release, we must allow time for folk tales of Jordan's dominance to start spreading. If his video game character matches M.J.'s real life greatness, he could catapult into elite video game athlete company.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="640">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/aIy9_558v3k?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">

             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>

             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             19. Allejo: International Superstar Soccer
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:195px">
            <img alt="19. Allejo: International Superstar Soccer" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/860/images_crop_195x258.jpg?1286919050" height="258" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="195"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Brazil's fictional soccer stud Allejo slipped through the cracks in the annals of video game athlete history, but his dominance must be recognized.
           </p>
           <p>
            Allejo's anonymity still hurts his stance on this list, but based on stories and video evidence, he might actually be worthy of a top ten spot. He broke free on breakaways almost every single time he had the ball, and goaltenders had little to no chance of stopping him.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/QRPf4gNWbIg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/QRPf4gNWbIg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             18. Christian Okoye: Tecmo Bowl
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:400px">
            <img alt="18. Christian Okoye: Tecmo Bowl" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/434/490/christianokoye_crop_400x266.jpg?1286821982" height="266" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="400"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Unlike some of the other Tecmo Bowl superstars on this list, Christian Okoye was a different breed. Rather than run around in circles, evading diving defenders, Okoye chose the straight ahead, bulldozer route.
           </p>
           <p>
            Okoye was nicknamed the Nigerian Nightmare not because he was guaranteed to shed four or five tackles on any given play, unless Lawrence Taylor was lining up against him. How many concussions did Tecmo Bowl Christian Okoye suffer? Enough to cut his career disappointingly short.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/T_ddO5ENtus?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/T_ddO5ENtus?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">
               52
              </span>
             </div>
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Next Page">
              Next
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             17. Mario Lemieux: NHL 94
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:600px">
            <img alt="17. Mario Lemieux: NHL 94" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/097/nhl_g_lemieux_600_crop_600x400.jpg?1286822277" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="600"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Mario Lemieux is considered by many as the best pound for pound hockey player of all time. Lemieux towered over Wayne Gretzky with his 6-foot-4, 235 pound frame. His size allowed him to wreak havoc in all aspects of the game, and provide a more dominating presence than the Great One.
           </p>
           <p>
            That real life dominance transferred directly into NHL '94 where Lemieux was a lock for multiple goals every game. He could fly down the ice, coast to coast, untouched, making opposing goaltenders his prey.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/jW2C3Qq9BVc?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/jW2C3Qq9BVc?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             16. Thomas Johansson: Virtua Tennis
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:279px">
            <img alt="16. Thomas Johansson: Virtua Tennis" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/441/001/sp1_crop_279x205.jpg?1286920679" height="205" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="279"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            In order for a tennis player to make this list, he had to be pretty darn special.
           </p>
           <p>
            An overbearing serve, powerful forehand, and insane court coverage allowed Thomas Johansson to do so. Whether controlled by human or computer, Johansson's agility made him incredibly difficult to defeat.
           </p>
           <p>
            Once he had you running from side to side on the court, you were doomed.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/YfadnkV-Xkg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/YfadnkV-Xkg?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-37 cf display-none " data-page="37">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             15. Ricky Henderson: RBI Baseball 4
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:467px">
            <img alt="15. Ricky Henderson: RBI Baseball 4" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/442/177/rickey-henderson_crop_467x312.jpg?1286982965" height="312" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="467"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            As we touched on earlier, there's one thing that remains true in sports video games: speed kills.
           </p>
           <p>
            In RBI Baseball 4, Rickey Henderson had speed, and power, and amazing contact skills. So long as Rickey put the ball in play, he was probably going to reach base. And once he was on base, he was probably going to steal second. And once he was on second he was probably going to steal third.
           </p>
           <p>
            Henderson's power made him the game's most valuable asset, and one of the best virtual baseball players of all time.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-38 cf display-none " data-page="38">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             14. Peyton Manning: Madden... Ever Year
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:590px">
            <img alt="14. Peyton Manning: Madden... Ever Year" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/434/423/madden-nfl-11-demo-20_crop_590x332.jpg?1286566533" height="332" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="590"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            We can all appreciate EA Sports and Madden's attempts to authenticate every facet of the NFL game experience, but if there's one thing that they could just ignore, it's the obnoxious pre-snap jabber of Peyton Manning.
           </p>
           <p>
            Everybody has played against Manning at some point or another, and cringed as he runs around the backfield, wearing the play clock down to one second, and then proceeding to toss a touchdown to Reggie Wayne behind your stingy cover 3 defense.
           </p>
           <p>
            Manning has been the NFL's most consistent player over the past decade, and that consistency has carried over into the video game world. He has a 99 overall rating virtually every year, and always makes for a great first round pick in Madden fantasy drafts.
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/ddceHQ1XQx8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/ddceHQ1XQx8?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-39 cf display-none " data-page="39">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             13. Jon Dowd: MVP Baseball 2005
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:460px">
            <img alt="13. Jon Dowd: MVP Baseball 2005" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/434/426/dowd1inline_1080859257_crop_460x345.jpg?1286566604" height="345" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="460"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Because Barry Bonds is a grumpy human being, he refused to join the MLBPA, therefore preventing his likeness from being used in any MLB licensed video games. In order to compensate for the home run king's absence, alter-egos were created.
           </p>
           <p>
            MLB 2K7 used "Joe Young" as a pseudonym for Bonds, and MLB 07 created "Reggie Stocker" in place of the slugger. However, both paled in comparison to the prowess of EA MVP Baseball's Jon Down.
           </p>
           <p>
            Dowd was constructed as a complete contrast to Bonds. He was white, right handed, and didn't use any of the military-issued armor that Bonds used to pack onto his right arm. When it came to baseball, though, Dowd was, like his alter-ego, flat out scary to pitch to. Few video game athletes actually threatened human pitchers like Dowd did in his day, and few video game baseball players took humans deep as many times as he did.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             12. Charles Barkley: Barkley Shut Up and Jam!
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:400px">
            <img alt="12. Charles Barkley: Barkley Shut Up and Jam!" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/440/975/608923_crop_400x300.jpg?1286919987" height="300" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="400"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Sir Charles might not have been the type of player to just "shut up" considering his big-mouth reputation, but his virtual athlete could jam.
           </p>
           <p>
            Barkley was a monster in his own game. He could roll over and steal the ball from anybody, deny any player going up for a dunk, and drive his way to the basket at will.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            <object height="385" width="480">
             <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/tlUjvlYLjIA?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US">
             </param>
             <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true">
             </param>
             <param name="allowscriptaccess" value="always">
             </param>
             <embed height="385" src="http://www.youtube.com/v/tlUjvlYLjIA?fs=1&amp;hl=en_US" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" width="480">
             </embed>
            </object>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             11. Reggie Jackson: RBI Baseball
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:286px">
            <img alt="11. Reggie Jackson: RBI Baseball" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/393/reggie.jackson.si_crop_286x420.jpg?1286829547" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="286"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Reggie Jackson spent the majority of his professional baseball career crushing home runs in baseball parks across the nation. That power followed him into the world of RBI Baseball.
           </p>
           <p>
            Mr. October was actually in the fading years of his career when RBI Baseball came out, but the then California Angel was the best player in the game. He could smash homers at will, and his batting skills are rivaled only by Jon Dowd and Ken Griffey, Jr.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             10. Randall Cunningham: Tecmo Bowl
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:576px">
            <img alt="10. Randall Cunningham: Tecmo Bowl" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/000/438/088/nfl_g_rcunningham1_576_crop_576x324.jpg?1286822109" height="324" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="576"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Randall Cunningham, also known as "QB Eagles" was Michael Vick before there was Michael Vick.
           </p>
           <p>
            Cunningham could seamlessly weave through the pocket and scramble for huge gains, and possess an equally impressive arm.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
